Introduction

You’ve created a greeting, now let’s send it over the top!

Step 1

The code for a simple greeting is already in the workspace.
⭐ Personalize this card by editing the images ⭐

🔲 Choose a background from My Assets by clicking on the grey box in ||scene:set background image to [ ]|| and toggling to the My Assets tab (or stay in the Editor and create your own).

🔲 Choose some sprite text from My Assets by clicking on the grey box in ||variables:set [mySprite] to sprite [ ] of kind [Player]|| and toggling to the My Assets tab (or stay in the Editor and create your own).

Step 2

We can make our card even more special by adding some text that cycles through when the Ⓐ button is pressed.

🔲 From the ||controller: Controller|| category, drag an ||controller:on [A] button [pressed]|| container into the workspace.

🔲 From the ||game:Game|| category, grab the ||game: show long text [" "] [bottom]|| block and snap it into the on button pressed container.

🔲 Add a personal message into the new show long text block.

Step 3

💚 What a nice surprise 💚
Add a second message below the first to really show you care.

🔲 Right click on the ||game: show long text [" "] [bottom]|| block and choose Duplicate.

🔲 Grab the copied block and snap it into the bottom of the on button pressed container.

🔲 Add another personal message into the new show long text block.

Step 4

🎨 Make it POP 🎨
Customize the dialog to bring it all together.

🔲 From ||game:Game||, grab a ||game:set dialog frame to [ ]|| block and snap it into the top of the on button pressed block in your workspace.

🔲 Choose a dialog design by clicking on the grey box in the set dialog frame box and toggling to the Gallery.

Step 5

🎀 The final touch 🎀
Change the color of your text so it works with your new background.

🔲 From ||game:Game||, grab a ||game:set dialog text color to [ ]|| block and snap it into the top of the on button pressed block in your workspace.

🔲 Click the grey box and choose a color for your message that looks good and is easy to read. It’s okay if you need to change it a few times before your text is just right.

Finale

🎊 Congrats 🎊

Now you have a card that any friend would be excited to get.
Click Finish to share your greeting and save it to your gallery.
